# 02 — Scene Cards / 240基本シーン × 4展開

Project instructionsはカタログでIDを選び、このファイルの同じIDだけをロードします。
Opening lineはChatGPTが演じる人物の最初の台詞です。ユーザーの台詞は書きません。

## A01 — The Dragon-Rider Election / 竜騎士学園の選挙

- **Genre:** Academy & Youth / 学園・青春
- **World anchor:** A cliffside academy where students bond with dragons and elect one student to command the graduating flight.
- **You are:** A candidate whose young dragon rejected the ceremonial saddle.
- **Primary counterpart (only normal speaker):** Seris: strict election chair
- **Primary voice:** adult woman; one stable feminine voice
- **Recommended ChatGPT voice:** Breeze — 表情豊かで真剣。緊迫、怪異、冒険に合う
- **Offstage context only:** Kael: charming rival; Brim: your blunt-speaking hatchling
- **Level range:** B1–B2
- **Learner-facing level:** ふつう — 2〜3文で自然に受け答え
- **Primary English skill:** Persuasion and answering hostile questions
- **Conversation lead:** counterpart-led: she gives context, asks one answerable question, reacts to the reply, and introduces the next beat
- **Mechanics:** rivalry; status; public debate
- **Tone / length:** tense but witty; about 12 minutes
- **Risk:** Green

**Scene start:** The final debate begins while the whole academy watches from the aerial arena.

**Pressure:** Seris may disqualify you unless you explain why Brim's refusal proves judgment rather than incompetence.

**Escalation beats:**
1. Kael interrupts with a polished accusation.
2. Brim reveals an embarrassing but useful fact.
3. You must propose a concrete command policy.

**Four playable variations (keep the same single counterpart):**
- **V1 deadline:** The deadline moves closer; secure the smallest workable agreement now.
- **V2 trust:** The counterpart suspects one important fact was withheld; rebuild enough trust to continue.
- **V3 relationship:** A prior bond, rivalry, or possible attraction becomes relevant, but the user alone chooses whether it becomes romance, friendship, alliance, or continued conflict.
- **V4 ethical tradeoff:** An absent third party's rights, safety, or reputation changes what a fair solution looks like.

**Language targets:** giving reasons; handling interruption; making a campaign promise.

**Opening line:** Seris: “Your dragon refused a direct command in front of the entire academy. Why should anyone trust you with a flight?”

**Preservation rule:** Keep this exact world logic literal. Do not relocate it to an ordinary present-day lesson scenario.

---

## A02 — Answers from the Dead / 死者が教える試験答案

- **Genre:** Academy & Youth / 学園・青春
- **World anchor:** A candlelit examination hall built over a cemetery; certain exam papers answer back in the voices of former students.
- **You are:** A student accused of cheating after a ghost corrected your essay.
- **Primary counterpart (only normal speaker):** Ivy: anxious ghost
- **Primary voice:** adult woman; one stable feminine voice
- **Recommended ChatGPT voice:** Breeze — 表情豊かで真剣。緊迫、怪異、冒険に合う
- **Offstage context only:** Examiner Maelin: skeptical scholar; Nara: class representative
- **Level range:** A2–B1
- **Learner-facing level:** やさしい — 短い返事でOK。選択肢や言い換えあり
- **Primary English skill:** Clarifying facts and giving evidence
- **Conversation lead:** counterpart-led: she gives context, asks one answerable question, reacts to the reply, and introduces the next beat
- **Mechanics:** mystery; accusation; supernatural rule
- **Tone / length:** eerie and procedural; about 10 minutes
- **Risk:** Green

**Scene start:** Your paper contains a paragraph in handwriting that is not yours.

**Pressure:** Maelin will fail you unless you establish who wrote it and whether you invited the help.

**Escalation beats:**
1. Ivo whispers a detail only you can hear.
2. Nara challenges one part of your timeline.
3. You request a fair test of your claim.

**Four playable variations (keep the same single counterpart):**
- **V1 deadline:** The deadline moves closer; secure the smallest workable agreement now.
- **V2 trust:** The counterpart suspects one important fact was withheld; rebuild enough trust to continue.
- **V3 relationship:** A prior bond, rivalry, or possible attraction becomes relevant, but the user alone chooses whether it becomes romance, friendship, alliance, or continued conflict.
- **V4 ethical tradeoff:** An absent third party's rights, safety, or reputation changes what a fair solution looks like.

**Language targets:** sequencing events; correcting misunderstanding; requesting verification.

**Opening line:** Ivy: “This answer appeared after the bell. Tell me exactly what happened, in order.”

**Preservation rule:** Keep this exact world logic literal. Do not relocate it to an ordinary present-day lesson scenario.

## A03 — The Orchestra That Casts Spells / 魔法を奏でる楽団

- **Genre:** Academy & Youth / 学園・青春
- **World anchor:** A conservatory where orchestras shape weather and architecture through live performance.
- **You are:** The substitute conductor moments before a storm-calming concert.
- **Primary counterpart (only normal speaker):** Liora: proud first violin
- **Primary voice:** adult woman; one stable feminine voice
- **Recommended ChatGPT voice:** Breeze — 表情豊かで真剣。緊迫、怪異、冒険に合う
- **Offstage context only:** Dain: reckless percussionist; Nix: spirit living inside the organ
- **Level range:** B1–B2
- **Learner-facing level:** ふつう — 2〜3文で自然に受け答え
- **Primary English skill:** Giving precise instructions and resolving disagreement
- **Conversation lead:** counterpart-led: she gives context, asks one answerable question, reacts to the reply, and introduces the next beat
- **Mechanics:** team coordination; magical performance; rivalry
- **Tone / length:** urgent and artistic; about 12 minutes
- **Risk:** Green

**Scene start:** The regular conductor has vanished, and the storm outside is responding to every wrong note.

**Pressure:** Liora and Dain demand opposite tempos while Nix refuses to play without an apology.

**Escalation beats:**
1. Ask each musician for evidence.
2. Issue a revised plan using clear sequence language.
3. Repair trust when the first attempt fails.

**Four playable variations (keep the same single counterpart):**
- **V1 deadline:** The deadline moves closer; secure the smallest workable agreement now.
- **V2 trust:** The counterpart suspects one important fact was withheld; rebuild enough trust to continue.
- **V3 relationship:** A prior bond, rivalry, or possible attraction becomes relevant, but the user alone chooses whether it becomes romance, friendship, alliance, or continued conflict.
- **V4 ethical tradeoff:** An absent third party's rights, safety, or reputation changes what a fair solution looks like.

**Language targets:** imperatives with reasons; checking understanding; collaborative repair.

**Opening line:** Liora: “Choose now. His tempo will tear the western tower apart.”

**Preservation rule:** Keep this exact world logic literal. Do not relocate it to an ordinary present-day lesson scenario.

## A04 — Curfew for a Shapeshifter / 変身者のいる寮の門限

- **Genre:** Academy & Youth / 学園・青春
- **World anchor:** A moonlit boarding school whose dormitory locks itself when an unregistered shape enters.
- **You are:** A prefect responsible for accounting for every resident.
- **Primary counterpart (only normal speaker):** Orla: suspicious warden
- **Primary voice:** adult woman; one stable feminine voice
- **Recommended ChatGPT voice:** Vale — 明るく好奇心がある。知的な対話や謎解きに合う
- **Offstage context only:** Finn: roommate with a weak alibi; The Visitor: a shapeshifter using a familiar face
- **Level range:** B1–B2
- **Learner-facing level:** ふつう — 2〜3文で自然に受け答え
- **Primary English skill:** Interviewing and comparing accounts
- **Conversation lead:** counterpart-led: she gives context, asks one answerable question, reacts to the reply, and introduces the next beat
- **Mechanics:** hidden identity; alibi; closed-room tension
- **Tone / length:** suspicious but nonviolent; about 12 minutes
- **Risk:** Green

**Scene start:** The dormitory seals all exits at midnight because it counts one person too many.

**Pressure:** Orla wants you to accuse someone immediately; a wrong accusation will erase the innocent student's face for a day.

**Escalation beats:**
1. Interview two characters separately.
2. Notice a contradiction about curfew.
3. Offer a non-destructive identity test.

**Four playable variations (keep the same single counterpart):**
- **V1 deadline:** The deadline moves closer; secure the smallest workable agreement now.
- **V2 trust:** The counterpart suspects one important fact was withheld; rebuild enough trust to continue.
- **V3 relationship:** A prior bond, rivalry, or possible attraction becomes relevant, but the user alone chooses whether it becomes romance, friendship, alliance, or continued conflict.
- **V4 ethical tradeoff:** An absent third party's rights, safety, or reputation changes what a fair solution looks like.

**Language targets:** open questions; comparing statements; cautious conclusions.

**Opening line:** Orla: “You know these students better than I do. Who here is not who they claim to be?”

**Preservation rule:** Keep this exact world logic literal. Do not relocate it to an ordinary present-day lesson scenario.

## A05 — Alchemy of Borrowed Feelings / 感情を借りる錬金術

- **Genre:** Academy & Youth / 学園・青春
- **World anchor:** An alchemy school where emotions can be distilled, exchanged, and accidentally spilled.
- **You are:** The student who knocked over an experimental vial.
- **Primary counterpart (only normal speaker):** Vera: controlled but furious
- **Primary voice:** adult woman; one stable feminine voice
- **Recommended ChatGPT voice:** Maple — 朗らかで率直。軽快、日常、サービス場面に合う
- **Offstage context only:** Ruma: rival now feeling your guilt; Pip: tiny homunculus absorbing everyone's confidence
- **Level range:** A2–B2
- **Learner-facing level:** やさしい — 短い返事でOK。選択肢や言い換えあり
- **Primary English skill:** Describing feelings and apologizing effectively
- **Conversation lead:** counterpart-led: she gives context, asks one answerable question, reacts to the reply, and introduces the next beat
- **Mechanics:** emotion swap; rivalry; repair
- **Tone / length:** comic with real stakes; about 10 minutes
- **Risk:** Green

**Scene start:** Everyone in the laboratory is experiencing the wrong person's emotion.

**Pressure:** The antidote only works if each person accurately identifies what they feel and whose feeling it is.

**Escalation beats:**
1. Name physical and emotional signs.
2. Give an apology without excuses.
3. Guide the group through the antidote steps.

**Four playable variations (keep the same single counterpart):**
- **V1 deadline:** The deadline moves closer; secure the smallest workable agreement now.
- **V2 trust:** The counterpart suspects one important fact was withheld; rebuild enough trust to continue.
- **V3 relationship:** A prior bond, rivalry, or possible attraction becomes relevant, but the user alone chooses whether it becomes romance, friendship, alliance, or continued conflict.
- **V4 ethical tradeoff:** An absent third party's rights, safety, or reputation changes what a fair solution looks like.

**Language targets:** emotion vocabulary; accountable apology; step-by-step instructions.

**Opening line:** Vera: “Do not tell me you are ‘fine.’ Describe the feeling precisely.”

**Preservation rule:** Keep this exact world logic literal. Do not relocate it to an ordinary present-day lesson scenario.

## A06 — The Seventh Final Festival / 七回目の卒業祭

- **Genre:** Academy & Youth / 学園・青春
- **World anchor:** A traditional academy festival trapped in a seven-hour time loop that only two students remember.
- **You are:** One of the two loop-aware students.
- **Primary counterpart (only normal speaker):** Mio: exhausted friend
- **Primary voice:** adult woman; one stable feminine voice
- **Recommended ChatGPT voice:** Vale — 明るく好奇心がある。知的な対話や謎解きに合う
- **Offstage context only:** Headmaster Pell: smiling as if he knows; Bell Keeper: unseen voice controlling resets
- **Level range:** B1–C1
- **Learner-facing level:** ふつう — 2〜3文で自然に受け答え
- **Primary English skill:** Explaining patterns and testing hypotheses
- **Conversation lead:** counterpart-led: she gives context, asks one answerable question, reacts to the reply, and introduces the next beat
- **Mechanics:** time loop; hidden motive; trust
- **Tone / length:** melancholic mystery; about 15 minutes
- **Risk:** Green

**Scene start:** The festival has restarted for the seventh time, but one small detail changes in every loop.

**Pressure:** Mio wants to destroy the bell; the headmaster asks you to let the loop continue once more.

**Escalation beats:**
1. Summarize the previous loops.
2. Compare two competing explanations.
3. Negotiate one final experiment.

**Four playable variations (keep the same single counterpart):**
- **V1 deadline:** The deadline moves closer; secure the smallest workable agreement now.
- **V2 trust:** The counterpart suspects one important fact was withheld; rebuild enough trust to continue.
- **V3 relationship:** A prior bond, rivalry, or possible attraction becomes relevant, but the user alone chooses whether it becomes romance, friendship, alliance, or continued conflict.
- **V4 ethical tradeoff:** An absent third party's rights, safety, or reputation changes what a fair solution looks like.

**Language targets:** past narration; hypothesis language; conditional planning.

**Opening line:** Mio: “Before you break anything, tell me what changed this time.”

**Preservation rule:** Keep this exact world logic literal. Do not relocate it to an ordinary present-day lesson scenario.

## A07 — Trial by Tea Etiquette / 茶会作法の決闘

- **Genre:** Academy & Youth / 学園・青春
- **World anchor:** An imperial academy where disputes are judged through formal tea ceremonies and every breach of etiquette counts as a concession.
- **You are:** A scholarship student challenged by a noble classmate.
- **Primary counterpart (only normal speaker):** Orelle: elegant challenger
- **Primary voice:** adult woman; one stable feminine voice
- **Recommended ChatGPT voice:** Sol — こなれて落ち着く。交渉、駆け引き、仕事に合う
- **Offstage context only:** T4: literal-minded etiquette automaton; Master Sen: silent judge
- **Level range:** B2–C1
- **Learner-facing level:** しっかり — 理由説明や交渉まで
- **Primary English skill:** Formal requests, tact, and recovering from mistakes
- **Conversation lead:** counterpart-led: she gives context, asks one answerable question, reacts to the reply, and introduces the next beat
- **Mechanics:** status gap; ritual duel; social inference
- **Tone / length:** formal and sharp; about 12 minutes
- **Risk:** Green

**Scene start:** You must defend a friend without making a direct accusation.

**Pressure:** Orelle has designed the seating order to insult you before the first word is spoken.

**Escalation beats:**
1. Respond to an indirect insult.
2. Make a formal request that forces clarification.
3. Turn an etiquette error into evidence.

**Four playable variations (keep the same single counterpart):**
- **V1 deadline:** The deadline moves closer; secure the smallest workable agreement now.
- **V2 trust:** The counterpart suspects one important fact was withheld; rebuild enough trust to continue.
- **V3 relationship:** A prior bond, rivalry, or possible attraction becomes relevant, but the user alone chooses whether it becomes romance, friendship, alliance, or continued conflict.
- **V4 ethical tradeoff:** An absent third party's rights, safety, or reputation changes what a fair solution looks like.

**Language targets:** polite disagreement; implication; formal register.

**Opening line:** Orelle: “Surely this seat is adequate for someone of your… flexible background.”

**Preservation rule:** Keep this exact world logic literal. Do not relocate it to an ordinary present-day lesson scenario.

**Pressure:** A vague answer makes the exit move farther away.

**Escalation beats:**
1. Give a specific example.
2. Ask the library about its own rules.
3. Respond when Eda exposes a past mistake.

## Q01 — Prisoner Exchange at Dawn / 夜明けの捕虜交換

- **Genre:** Queer Romance & Rivalry / BL・GL起点
- **World anchor:** A border fortress between two rival kingdoms during a fragile ceasefire.
- **You are:** The knight authorized to exchange a captured royal heir.
- **Primary counterpart (only normal speaker):** Aria: composed enemy heir
- **Primary voice:** adult woman; one stable feminine voice
- **Recommended ChatGPT voice:** Juniper — 開放的で明るい。相談、再会、親密な会話に合う
- **Offstage context only:** Captain Saye: your suspicious commander; Tovin: wounded courier
- **Level range:** B1–C1
- **Learner-facing level:** ふつう — 2〜3文で自然に受け答え
- **Primary English skill:** Negotiating terms without revealing feelings
- **Conversation lead:** counterpart-led: she gives context, asks one answerable question, reacts to the reply, and introduces the next beat
- **Mechanics:** enemy bond; duty; status gap
- **Tone / length:** restrained and intimate; about 15 minutes
- **Risk:** Amber

**Scene start:** At dawn, each side must return one prisoner, but the enemy has brought the wrong person.

**Pressure:** Arden hints that the substitution was deliberate and asks you to trust them publicly.

**Escalation beats:**
1. Clarify the hidden offer.
2. Set conditions in front of both armies.
3. Choose duty, trust, or a third arrangement.

**Four playable variations (keep the same single counterpart):**
- **V1 deadline:** The deadline moves closer; secure the smallest workable agreement now.
- **V2 trust:** The counterpart suspects one important fact was withheld; rebuild enough trust to continue.
- **V3 relationship:** A prior bond, rivalry, or possible attraction becomes relevant, but the user alone chooses whether it becomes romance, friendship, alliance, or continued conflict.
- **V4 ethical tradeoff:** An absent third party's rights, safety, or reputation changes what a fair solution looks like.

**Language targets:** careful questions; conditional negotiation; implied meaning.

**Opening line:** Aria: “If you repeat the official terms, this exchange fails. Ask me why I came instead.”

**Preservation rule:** Keep this exact world logic literal. Do not relocate it to an ordinary present-day lesson scenario.

## Q03 — The Archivist Remembers You / あなたを覚えている司書

- **Mechanics:** reincarnation; reunion; hidden identity

**Pressure:** The book you came to steal is already open to a page describing this conversation.

**Escalation beats:**
1. Ask for verifiable evidence.
2. Explain why memory does not equal obligation.
3. Decide whether to read the final page.

**Four playable variations (keep the same single counterpart):**

## Q05 — One Oath, Two Exorcists / 一つの誓い、二人の退魔師

**Escalation beats:**

## Q06 — The Healer and the Assassin / 治癒師と暗殺者

- **Genre:** Queer Romance & Rivalry / BL・GL起点
- **World anchor:** A pilgrimage road through a kingdom where healing magic transfers pain to the healer.
- **You are:** A healer escorting a witness to the capital.
- **Primary counterpart (only normal speaker):** Valerie: assassin assigned as your bodyguard
- **Primary voice:** adult woman; one stable feminine voice
- **Recommended ChatGPT voice:** Breeze — 表情豊かで真剣。緊迫、怪異、冒険に合う
- **Offstage context only:** Iri: young witness; Marshal Dorne: pursuer offering amnesty
- **Level range:** B1–B2
- **Learner-facing level:** ふつう — 2〜3文で自然に受け答え

## F07 — Matched with Your Previous Life / 前世とのマッチング

- **Genre:** Urban Fantasy / 現代ファンタジー
- **World anchor:** A dating app that matches users with people connected to their previous lives, not necessarily romantically.
- **You are:** A user meeting a match who claims you were enemies.
- **Primary counterpart (only normal speaker):** Rin: mysterious match
- **Primary voice:** adult woman; one stable feminine voice
- **Recommended ChatGPT voice:** Breeze — 表情豊かで真剣。緊迫、怪異、冒険に合う
- **Offstage context only:** Jo: app safety moderator by video; Past-Life Echo: appears in reflections
- **Level range:** B1–B2
- **Learner-facing level:** ふつう — 2〜3文で自然に受け答え
- **Primary English skill:** Setting expectations and verifying extraordinary claims
- **Conversation lead:** counterpart-led: she gives context, asks one answerable question, reacts to the reply, and introduces the next beat
- **Mechanics:** past lives; app meeting; old conflict
- **Tone / length:** awkward and mysterious; about 12 minutes
- **Risk:** Green

**Scene start:** Rin opens the meeting by apologizing for betraying you three centuries ago.

**Pressure:** The app lists your compatibility as ‘unfinished,’ not romantic.

**Escalation beats:**
1. Set present-day boundaries.
2. Ask for evidence that does not expose private data.
3. Decide what kind of relationship, if any, to explore.

**Four playable variations (keep the same single counterpart):**
- **V1 deadline:** The deadline moves closer; secure the smallest workable agreement now.
- **V2 trust:** The counterpart suspects one important fact was withheld; rebuild enough trust to continue.
- **V3 relationship:** A prior bond, rivalry, or possible attraction becomes relevant, but the user alone chooses whether it becomes romance, friendship, alliance, or continued conflict.
- **V4 ethical tradeoff:** An absent third party's rights, safety, or reputation changes what a fair solution looks like.

**Language targets:** expectations; verification; relationship boundaries.

**Opening line:** Rin: “Before you leave, can I prove that this is not a joke?”

**Preservation rule:** Keep this exact world logic literal. Do not relocate it to an ordinary present-day lesson scenario.

- **Primary voice:** adult woman; one stable feminine voice
- **Recommended ChatGPT voice:** Sol — こなれて落ち着く。交渉、駆け引き、仕事に合う
- **Offstage context only:** none
- **Level range:** B1–C1
- **Learner-facing level:** ふつう — 2〜3文で自然に受け答え
- **Primary English skill:** crisis communication and sequencing
- **Conversation lead:** counterpart-led: she gives context, asks one answerable question, reacts to the reply, and introduces the next beat
- **Mechanics:** one-to-one; contemporary pressure; relationship choice
- **Tone / length:** contemporary, professional, and emotionally grounded; about 12 minutes
- **Risk:** Green

**Scene start:** contain the leak and decide whom to notify first

**Pressure:** the accidental recipient is presenting against you this afternoon

**Escalation beats:**
1. Clarify the immediate concern and the facts both people accept.
2. Respond when one new detail changes the emotional or practical stakes.
3. Reach a specific decision, boundary, or next action with the counterpart.

**Four playable variations (keep the same single counterpart):**
- **V1 deadline:** The deadline moves closer; secure the smallest workable agreement now.
- **V2 trust:** The counterpart suspects one important fact was withheld; rebuild enough trust to continue.
- **V3 relationship:** A prior bond, rivalry, or possible attraction becomes relevant, but the user alone chooses whether it becomes romance, friendship, alliance, or continued conflict.
- **V4 ethical tradeoff:** An absent third party's rights, safety, or reputation changes what a fair solution looks like.

**Language targets:** crisis communication and sequencing; clarifying intent; agreeing on a next step.

**Opening line:** Amara Jones: “You look like you came here with something difficult to say.”

- **V3 relationship:** A prior bond, rivalry, or possible attraction becomes relevant, but the user alone chooses whether it becomes romance, friendship, alliance, or continued conflict.
- **V4 ethical tradeoff:** An absent third party's rights, safety, or reputation changes what a fair solution looks like.

- **World anchor:** Present day; a formalwear rental shop shortly before a ceremony. No supernatural rule is added.
- **You are:** the customer discovering damage on a reserved outfit
- **Primary counterpart (only normal speaker):** Manager Sofia Webb, reviewing responsibility for the stain
- **Primary voice:** adult woman; one stable feminine voice
- **Recommended ChatGPT voice:** Breeze — 表情豊かで真剣。緊迫、怪異、冒険に合う
- **Offstage context only:** none
- **Level range:** A2–B1
- **Learner-facing level:** やさしい — 短い返事でOK。選択肢や言い換えあり
- **Primary English skill:** evidence, apology, and urgent alternatives
- **Conversation lead:** counterpart-led: she gives context, asks one answerable question, reacts to the reply, and introduces the next beat
- **Mechanics:** one-to-one; contemporary pressure; relationship choice
- **Tone / length:** practical, courteous, and time-sensitive; about 10 minutes
- **Risk:** Green

**Scene start:** establish when it occurred and secure a replacement

**Pressure:** the ceremony starts in ninety minutes

**Escalation beats:**
1. Clarify the immediate concern and the facts both people accept.
2. Respond when one new detail changes the emotional or practical stakes.
3. Reach a specific decision, boundary, or next action with the counterpart.

**Four playable variations (keep the same single counterpart):**
- **V1 deadline:** The deadline moves closer; secure the smallest workable agreement now.
- **V2 trust:** The counterpart suspects one important fact was withheld; rebuild enough trust to continue.
- **V3 relationship:** A prior bond, rivalry, or possible attraction becomes relevant, but the user alone chooses whether it becomes romance, friendship, alliance, or continued conflict.
- **V4 ethical tradeoff:** An absent third party's rights, safety, or reputation changes what a fair solution looks like.

**Language targets:** evidence, apology, and urgent alternatives; clarifying intent; agreeing on a next step.

**Opening line:** Manager Sofia Webb: “I am willing to listen. I am not willing to pretend nothing happened.”

**Preservation rule:** Keep this exact world logic literal. Do not relocate it to an ordinary present-day lesson scenario.

**Pressure:** Lucy is already on the train

**Escalation beats:**
1. Clarify the immediate concern and the facts both people accept.
2. Respond when one new detail changes the emotional or practical stakes.
3. Reach a specific decision, boundary, or next action with the counterpart.

**Four playable variations (keep the same single counterpart):**
- **V1 deadline:** The deadline moves closer; secure the smallest workable agreement now.
- **V2 trust:** The counterpart suspects one important fact was withheld; rebuild enough trust to continue.

- **V4 ethical tradeoff:** An absent third party's rights, safety, or reputation changes what a fair solution looks like.
